NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICES
Tamil Nadu Chemists and Allied Distributors Alliance Limited
(under Liquidation)
Old No. 82, New No. 16C, 4th Main Road, Gandhi Nagar, Adyar, Chennai-600 020.
Notice of resolution passed by the members for voluntary winding-up
[pursuant to Section 485 of Companies Act, 1956]
Notice is hereby given that, the members of Tamil Nadu Chemists and Allied Distributors Alliance Limited
(under Liquidation) have passed the following special resolution for voluntary winding-up of the company, at the
Extraordinary General Meeting held on Tuesday, 24th September 2013 at 4.45 P.M.
“Resolved that pursuant to Section 484 and other applicable provisions of the Companies Act, 1956, the
company, being solvent and in a position to meet all its debts and liabilities in full, be voluntarily wound-up.”
Chennai,
18th October 2013.

B. ARUMUGAM,
Chairman.

GEO FABRICS INDIA PRIVATE LIMITED
53, (Old No. 27), 1st Main Road, G-1, Sneha Apartments, Ground Floor, R.A. Puram, Chennai-600 028.
NOTICE is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 of the Companies Act, 1956, that a General Meeting of the
members of the above named company will be held at the registered office of the company at 53, (Old No. 27), 1st Main
Road, G-1, Sneha Apartments, Ground Floor, R.A. Puram, Chennai, Tamil Nadu-600 028 at 11.30 A.M. on Monday
the 25th November 2013 for the purpose of having an account laid before them showing the manner in which the winding
up has been conducted and the property of the company disposed off and for hearing any explanation that may be given
by the liquidator and also for determining by a special resolution of the Company, the manner in which the books of the
accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator shall be disposed off.
Chennai,
18th October 2013.

S. SANDEEP,
Liquidator of the Company.
